 205  DNTotCost.. DNObjFunc =e= sum(y, ( InvCost(y) + OprCost(y) + LossCost(y))/
      ((1+roi)**YY(y)))  ;
 206   
 207  eq_InvCost(y)..  InvCost(y) =e= sum(S_can, (Z1(S_can,y)-Z1(S_can,y-1))*nod
      e_data(S_can,'NIC1') + (Z2(S_can,y)-Z2(S_can,y-1))*node_data(S_can,'NIC2')
      )
 208  +sum(np,(ZR(np,y)-ZR(np,y-1))*node_data(np,'NRC'))+ sum(L_ex,(XR(L_ex,y)-X
      R(L_ex,y-1))*Line_data(L_ex,"LRC"))
 209  + sum(L_can,(XI1(L_can,y)-XI1(L_can,y-1))*Line_data(L_can,"LIC1"))
 210  + sum(L_can,(XI2(L_can,y)-XI2(L_can,y-1))*Line_data(L_can,"LIC2"))
 211  + sum(L_can,(XI3(L_can,y)-XI3(L_can,y-1))*Line_data(L_can,"LIC3")) ;
 212   
 213  eq_OprCost(y).. OprCost(y) =e= sum(S_can,Z1(S_can,y)*node_data(S_can,'Psma
      x1')*SubOC + Z2(S_can,y)*node_data(S_can,'PSmax2')*SubOC)
 214  + sum(S_ex,node_data(S_ex,'Psmax')*SubOC) +  sum(n, rp(n,y)*LOLEcost) ;
 215   
 216  eq_LossCost(y).. LossCost(y) =e= sum(L_ex, Lf*PFlin(L_ex,y)*Line_data(L_ex
      ,'R')*LossCost_C)
 217  + sum(L_can, Lf*PFlin(L_can,y)*Line_data(L_can,'R')*LossCost_C) ;
 218  *eq_Salvage.. SalvageCost =e= sum(S_ex,XR(S_ex,'y7')) + sum(S_can,XI(S_can
      ,'y7'))
 219  *eq_Revenue(y).. Revenue(y) =e= price_en(y)*sum(n,LoadP_data(n,y) - rp(n,y
      )) ;
 220  *KCL:    r(n,t) is load not served.
 221   
 222  eq_lin1(l,y).. PFlin(l,y) =e= uu(l,y) + vv(l,y);
 223  eq_lin2(l,y).. PF(l,y) =e= uu(l,y) - vv(l,y) ;
 224  eq_lin3(l,y).. uu(l,y) =l= M*b(l,y) ;
 225  eq_lin4(l,y).. vv(l,y) =l= M*(1-b(l,y)) ;
 226   
 227  KCL(n,y).. Pprod(n,y) + rp(n,y) +  sum(L$(Line_data(L,'tbus')=numn(n)),PF(
      L,y)) =e=  sum(L$(Line_data(L,'fbus')=numn(n)),PF(L,y)) + LoadP_data(n,y) 
      ;
 228   
 229  *KVL:   constraints are designed in a way to be relaxed when line is not i
      n use.
 230  * A /v1 is missing in KVL
 231  KVL1(L_ex,y).. sum(n,A(L_ex,n)*V(n,y)) =e= -(PF(L_ex,y)*Line_data(L_ex,"R"
      ) + QF(L_ex,y)*Line_data(L_ex,"X"))/Vref ;
 232  KVL21(L_can,y).. sum(n,A(L_can,n)*V(n,y)) + (PF(L_can,y)*Line_data(L_can,"
      R1") + QF(L_can,y)*Line_data(L_can,"X1"))/Vref =g= (XI1(L_can,y) - 1)*M  ;
 233  KVL22(L_can,y).. sum(n,A(L_can,n)*V(n,y)) + (PF(L_can,y)*Line_data(L_can,"
      R1") + QF(L_can,y)*Line_data(L_can,"X1"))/Vref =l= (1 - XI1(L_can,y))*M  ;
 234  KVL31(L_can,y).. sum(n,A(L_can,n)*V(n,y)) + (PF(L_can,y)*Line_data(L_can,"
      R2") + QF(L_can,y)*Line_data(L_can,"X2"))/Vref =g= (XI2(L_can,y) - 1)*M  ;
 235  KVL32(L_can,y).. sum(n,A(L_can,n)*V(n,y)) + (PF(L_can,y)*Line_data(L_can,"
      R2") + QF(L_can,y)*Line_data(L_can,"X2"))/Vref =l= (1 - XI2(L_can,y))*M  ;
 236  KVL41(L_can,y).. sum(n,A(L_can,n)*V(n,y)) + (PF(L_can,y)*Line_data(L_can,"
      R3") + QF(L_can,y)*Line_data(L_can,"X3"))/Vref =g= (XI3(L_can,y) - 1)*M  ;
 237  KVL42(L_can,y).. sum(n,A(L_can,n)*V(n,y)) + (PF(L_can,y)*Line_data(L_can,"
      R3") + QF(L_can,y)*Line_data(L_can,"X3"))/Vref =l= (1 - XI3(L_can,y))*M  ;
 238   
 239  *power flow limitations
 240  eq_powerflow1(L_ex,y).. PFlin(L_ex,y) =l= Line_data(L_ex,'PFmax') *(1 - XR
      (L_ex,y)) + Line_data(L_ex,'PFRmax')*XR(L_ex,y)  ;
 241  eq_powerflow2(L_can,y).. PFlin(L_can,y) =l= Line_data(L_can,'PFI1max')*XI1
      (L_can,y) + Line_data(L_can,'PFI2max')*XI2(L_can,y)
 242  + Line_data(L_can,'PFI3max')*XI3(L_can,y) ;
 243  eq_Qflow(L,y).. QF(L,y) =e= 0.75*PFlin(L,y) ;
 244   
 245  *to model Substation placing. Ppmax is zero for non-substations.
 246   
 247  eq_sub_ins(S_can,y).. Pprod(S_can,y) =l=  Z1(S_can,y)*node_data(S_can,'Psm
      ax1') + Z2(S_can,y)*node_data(S_can,'Psmax2') ;
 248  eq_OnlySub(S_can,y).. Z1(S_can,y) + Z2(S_can,y) =l= 1 ;
 249  *same model for existing substations replacement.
 250  eq_exSub1(np,y).. Pprod(np,y) =l= (1 - ZR(np,y))*node_data(np,'Psmax') + Z
      R(np,y)*node_data(np,'PsmaxR')  ;
 251  *eq_exSub2(S_ex,y).. Qprod(S_ex,y) =l= (1 - ZR(S_ex,y))*node_data(S_ex,'Qs
      max') + ZR(S_ex,y)*node_data(S_ex,'QsmaxR')  ;
 252  eq_exSub2(n,y).. Qprod(n,y) =e= 0.75*Pprod(n,y)  ;
 253   
 254  *to ensure only one replacement or installation
 255  eq_Line_rep(L_ex,y).. XR(L_ex,y) =g= XR(L_ex,y-1) ;
 256  eq_Line_ins1(L_can,y).. XI1(L_can,y) =g= XI1(L_can,y-1) ;
 257  eq_Line_ins2(L_can,y).. XI2(L_can,y) =g= XI2(L_can,y-1) ;
 258  eq_Line_ins3(L_can,y).. XI3(L_can,y) =g= XI3(L_can,y-1) ;
 259  eq_only_ins(L_can,y).. XI1(L_can,y) + XI2(L_can,y) + XI3(L_can,y) =l= 1 ;
 260   
 261  *eq_OnlyRep2(L_can).. sum(t,XI(L_can,y)) =l= 1 ;
 262   
 263  eq_ZOnce1(S_can,y).. Z1(S_can,y) =g= Z1(S_can,y-1) ;
 264  eq_ZOnce2(S_can,y).. Z2(S_can,y) =g= Z2(S_can,y-1) ;
 265  eq_OnlySubIns(S_can,y).. Z1(S_can,y) + Z2(S_can,y) =l= 1 ;
 266   
 267  eq_ZR(np,y).. ZR(np,y) =l= node_data(np,'state') ;
 268  eq_ZROnce(np,y).. ZR(np,y) =g= ZR(np,y-1) ;
 269   
 270   
 271  *Node Voltage limitations
 272  eq_referenceV(S,y).. V(S,y) =e= Vref ;
 273  *eq_Vmax(np,y).. V(np,y) =l= Node_data(np,"Vmax") ;
 274  *eq_Vmin(np,y).. V(np,y) =g= Node_data(np,"Vmin") ;
 275   
 276   
 277  Radiality1(y).. card(L_ex) + sum(L_can, XI1(L_can,y) + XI2(L_can,y) + XI3(
      L_can,y)) =e= number_of_nodes(y) -card(S_ex) ;
 278  Radiality2(n,y).. sum(L_can$(Line_data(L_can,"tbus")=ord(n)), XI1(L_can,y)
       + XI2(L_can,y) + XI3(L_can,y))
 279  + sum(L_ex$(Line_data(L_ex,"tbus")=ord(n)), Line_data(L_ex,'InitState')) =
      l= 1 ;
 280   
 281  display LoadP_data
 282  model DNPlanning /all/ ;
 283  option optcr = 0.01 ;
 284  option resLim = 1000000 ;
 285  solve DNPlanning minimizing DNObjFunc using mip;
 286

---- eq_InvCost  =E=  

eq_InvCost(y1)..  InvCost(y1) - 8500*XI1(l10,y1) - 8500*XI1(l11,y1)
     
      - 8500*XI1(l12,y1) - 8500*XI1(l13,y1) - 8500*XI1(l14,y1)
